  [2mDetails:[22m

  1. [1mCrash Location[22m: Line 26 in [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m function:
  [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores] = score;[39m
  2. [1mError Type[22m: EXC_BAD_ACCESS (code=1, address=0x0) - attempting to write
   to address 0x0 (NULL)
  3. [1mRoot Cause[22m: The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field in the Student structure is NULL
  (0x0000000000000000) but the code attempts to write to it as if it were a
   valid array.
  4. [1mVariable State at Crash[22m:
    - Student pointer [38;2;177;185;249ms[39m: Valid (0x000000011fe05580)
    - Student name: "Alice"
    - Student age: 20
    - [1mStudent scores[22m: NULL (0x0000000000000000) ← [1mThis is the problem[22m
    - Student num_scores: 0
  5. [1mCall Stack[22m: main() → add_score() → crash

  The bug is that the [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array was never allocated memory before
  attempting to write to it. The program should allocate memory for the
  scores array (likely using [38;2;177;185;249mmalloc[39m) before trying to store score values in
   it.
